class="docMainContainer_a9sJ"><div class="container padding-top--md padding-bottom--lg"><div class="row"><div class="col docItemCol_Qr34"><div class="docItemContainer_tjFy"><article><nav class="theme-doc-breadcrumbs breadcrumbsContainer_T5ub" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a aria-label="Home page" class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="breadcrumbHomeIcon_sfvy"><path d="M10 19v-5h4v5c0 .55.45 1 1 1h3c.55 0 1-.45 1-1v-7h1.7c.46 0 .68-.57.33-.87L12.67 3.6c-.38-.34-.96-.34-1.34 0l-8.36 7.53c-.34.3-.13.87.33.87H5v7c0 .55.45 1 1 1h3c.55 0 1-.45 1-1z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/docs/providers/"><span>Providers</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item breadcrumbs__item--active"><span class="breadcrumbs__link">AWS Bedrock</span></li></ul></nav><div class="tocCollapsible_wXna theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_Ojys"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_iI2p">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><div style="position:relative"><header><h1>Bedrock</h1></header>
<p>The <code>bedrock</code> provider lets you use Amazon Bedrock in your evals. This is a common way to access Anthropic&#x27;s Claude, Meta&#x27;s Llama 3.3, Amazon&#x27;s Nova, OpenAI&#x27;s GPT-OSS models, AI21&#x27;s Jamba, Alibaba&#x27;s Qwen, and other models. The complete list of available models can be found in the <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/bedrock/latest/userguide/model-ids.html#model-ids-arns" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">AWS Bedrock model IDs documentation</a>.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="setup">Setup<a href="#setup" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Setup" title="Direct link to Setup" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<ol>
<li class="">
<p><strong>Model Access</strong>: Amazon Bedrock provides automatic access to serverless foundation models with no manual approval required.</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Most models</strong>: Amazon, DeepSeek, Mistral, Meta, Qwen, and OpenAI models (including GPT-OSS and Qwen3) are available immediately - just start using them</li>
<li class=""><strong>Anthropic models</strong>: Require one-time use case submission through the model catalog (access granted immediately after submission)</li>
<li class=""><strong>AWS Marketplace models</strong>: Some third-party models require IAM permissions with <code>aws-marketplace:Subscribe</code></li>
<li class=""><strong>Access control</strong>: Organizations maintain control through IAM policies and Service Control Policies (SCPs)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="">
<p>Install the <code>@aws-sdk/client-bedrock-runtime</code> package:</p>
<div class="language-sh codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-sh codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">npm</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">install</span><span class="token plain"> @aws-sdk/client-bedrock-runtime</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
</li>
<li class="">
<p>The AWS SDK will automatically pull credentials from the following locations:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">IAM roles on EC2</li>
<li class=""><code>~/.aws/credentials</code></li>
<li class=""><code>AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID</code> and <code>AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY</code> environment variables</li>
</ul>
<p>See <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/sdk-for-javascript/v2/developer-guide/setting-credentials-node.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">setting node.js credentials (AWS)</a> for more details.</p>
</li>
<li class="">
<p>Edit your configuration file to point to the AWS Bedrock provider. Here&#x27;s an example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us.anthropic.claude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">4</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20250929</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v1</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Note that the provider is <code>bedrock:</code> followed by the <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/bedrock/latest/userguide/model-ids.html#model-ids-arns" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">ARN/model id</a> of the model.</p>
</li>
<li class="">
<p>Additional config parameters are passed like so:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">anthropic.claude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">3</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20241022</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v2</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">accessKeyId</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> YOUR_ACCESS_KEY_ID</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">secretAccessKey</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> YOUR_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">region</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;us-west-2&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">256</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="application-inference-profiles">Application Inference Profiles<a href="#application-inference-profiles" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Application Inference Profiles" title="Direct link to Application Inference Profiles" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>AWS Bedrock supports Application Inference Profiles, which allow you to use a single ARN to access multiple foundation models across different regions. This helps optimize costs and availability while maintaining consistent performance.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="using-inference-profiles">Using Inference Profiles<a href="#using-inference-profiles" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Using Inference Profiles" title="Direct link to Using Inference Profiles" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>When using an inference profile ARN, you must specify the <code>inferenceModelType</code> in your configuration to indicate which model family the profile is configured for:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">arn</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">aws</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">east</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">1</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">123456789012</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">application</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">inference</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">profile/my</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">profile</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">inferenceModelType</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;claude&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Required for inference profiles</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">region</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;us-east-1&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">256</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="supported-model-types">Supported Model Types<a href="#supported-model-types" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Supported Model Types" title="Direct link to Supported Model Types" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>The <code>inferenceModelType</code> config option supports the following values:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>claude</code> - For Anthropic Claude models</li>
<li class=""><code>nova</code> - For Amazon Nova models (v1)</li>
<li class=""><code>nova2</code> - For Amazon Nova 2 models (with reasoning support)</li>
<li class=""><code>llama</code> - Defaults to Llama 4 (latest version)</li>
<li class=""><code>llama2</code> - For Meta Llama 2 models</li>
<li class=""><code>llama3</code> - For Meta Llama 3 models</li>
<li class=""><code>llama3.1</code> or <code>llama3_1</code> - For Meta Llama 3.1 models</li>
<li class=""><code>llama3.2</code> or <code>llama3_2</code> - For Meta Llama 3.2 models</li>
<li class=""><code>llama3.3</code> or <code>llama3_3</code> - For Meta Llama 3.3 models</li>
<li class=""><code>llama4</code> - For Meta Llama 4 models</li>
<li class=""><code>mistral</code> - For Mistral models</li>
<li class=""><code>cohere</code> - For Cohere models</li>
<li class=""><code>ai21</code> - For AI21 models</li>
<li class=""><code>titan</code> - For Amazon Titan models</li>
<li class=""><code>deepseek</code> - For DeepSeek models</li>
<li class=""><code>openai</code> - For OpenAI models</li>
<li class=""><code>qwen</code> - For Alibaba Qwen models</li>
</ul>

plain">inference</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">profile/nova</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">profile</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">inferenceModelType</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;nova&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">interfaceConfig</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_new_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1024</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_WCGJ alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>tip</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Application Inference Profiles provide several benefits:</p><ul>
<li class=""><strong>Automatic failover</strong>: If one region is unavailable, requests automatically route to another region</li>
<li class=""><strong>Cost optimization</strong>: Routes to the most cost-effective available model</li>
<li class=""><strong>Simplified management</strong>: Use a single ARN instead of managing multiple model IDs</li>
</ul><p>When using inference profiles, ensure the <code>inferenceModelType</code> matches the model family your profile is configured for, as the configuration parameters differ between model types.</p></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="converse-api">Converse API<a href="#converse-api" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Converse API" title="Direct link to Converse API" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>The Converse API provides a unified interface across all Bedrock models with native support for extended thinking (reasoning), tool calling, and guardrails. Use the <code>bedrock:converse:</code> prefix to access this API.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="basic-usage">Basic Usage<a href="#basic-usage" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Basic Usage" title="Direct link to Basic Usage" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v2</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" us</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">east</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token number" <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="extended-thinking">Extended Thinking<a href="#extended-thinking" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Extended Thinking" title="Direct link to Extended Thinking" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Enable Claude&#x27;s extended thinking capabilities for complex reasoning tasks:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">converse</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us.anthropic.claude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">4</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20250929</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v1</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">region</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> us</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">west</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">2</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">maxTokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">20000</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">thinking</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> enabled</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">budget_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">16000</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">showThinking</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean important" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Include thinking content in output</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The <code>thinking</code> configuration controls Claude&#x27;s reasoning behavior:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>type: enabled</code> - Activates extended thinking</li>
<li class=""><code>budget_tokens</code> - Maximum tokens allocated for thinking (minimum 1024)</li>
</ul>
<p>Use <code>showThinking: true</code> to include the model&#x27;s reasoning process in the output, or <code>false</code> to only show the final response.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-warning admonition_WCGJ alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>warning</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Do not set <code>temperature</code>, <code>topP</code>, or <code>topK</code> when using extended thinking. These sampling parameters are incompatible with reasoning mode.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="configuration-options">Configuration Options<a href="#configuration-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Configuration Options" title="Direct link to Configuration Options" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<table><thead><tr><th>Option</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>maxTokens</code></td><td>Maximum output tokens</td></tr><tr><td><code>temperature</code></td><td>Sampling temperature (0-1)</td></tr><tr><td><code>topP</code></td><td>Nucleus sampling parameter</td></tr><tr><td><code>stopSequences</code></td><td>Array of stop sequences</td></tr><tr><td><code>thinking</code></td><td>Extended thinking configuration (Claude models)</td></tr><tr><td><code>reasoningConfig</code></td><td>Reasoning configuration (Amazon Nova 2 models)</td></tr><tr><td><code>showThinking</code></td><td>Include thinking in output (default: false)</td></tr><tr><td><code>performanceConfig</code></td><td>Performance settings (<code>latency: optimized</code>)</td></tr><tr><td><code>serviceTier</code></td><td>Service tier (<code>priority</code>, <code>default</code>, or <code>flex</code>)</td></tr><tr><td><code>guardrailIdentifier</code></td><td>Guardrail ID for content filtering</td></tr><tr><td><code>guardrailVersion</code></td><td>Guardrail version (default: DRAFT)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="performance-configuration">Performance Configuration<a href="#performance-configuration" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Performance Configuration" title="Direct link to Performance Configuration" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Optimize for latency or cost:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">performanceConfig</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="supported-models">Supported Models<a href="#supported-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Supported Models" title="Direct link to Supported Models" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>The Converse API works with all Bedrock models that support the Converse operation:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Claude</strong>: All Claude 3.x and 4.x models</li>
<li class=""><strong>Amazon Nova</strong>: Lite, Micro, Pro, Premier (not Sonic)</li>
<li class=""><strong>Amazon Nova 2</strong>: Lite (with reasoning support)</li>
<li class=""><strong>Meta Llama</strong>: 3.x, 4.x models</li>
<li class=""><strong>Mistral</strong>: All Mistral models</li>
<li class=""><strong>Cohere</strong>: Command R and R+ models</li>
<li class=""><strong>AI21</strong>: Jamba models</li>
<li class=""><strong>DeepSeek</strong>: R1 and other models</li>
<li class=""><strong>Qwen</strong>: Qwen3 models</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="authentication">Authentication<a href="#authentication" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Authentication" title="Direct link to Authentication" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>Amazon Bedrock supports multiple authentication methods, including the new API key authentication for simplified access. Credentials are resolved in this priority order:</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="credential-resolution-order">Credential Resolution Order<a href="#credential-resolution-order" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Credential Resolution Order" title="Direct link to Credential Resolution Order" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Credentials are resolved in the following priority order:</p>
<ol>
<li class=""><strong>Explicit credentials in config</strong> (<code>accessKeyId</code>, <code>secretAccessKey</code>)</li>
<li class=""><strong>Bedrock API Key authentication</strong> (<code>apiKey</code>)</li>
<li class=""><strong>SSO profile authentication</strong> (<code>profile</code>)</li>
<li class=""><strong>AWS default credential chain</strong> (environment variables, <code>~/.aws/credentials</code>)</li>
</ol>
<p>The first available credential method is used automatically.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="authentication-options">Authentication Options<a href="#authentication-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Authentication Options" title="Direct link to Authentication Options" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="1-explicit-credentials-highest-priority">1. Explicit credentials (highest priority)<a href="#1-explicit-credentials-highest-priority" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to 1. Explicit credentials (highest priority)" title="Direct link to 1. Explicit credentials (highest priority)" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>Specify AWS access keys directly in your configuration. <strong>For security, use environment variables instead of hardcoding credentials:</strong></p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us.anthropic.claude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">3</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20241022</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v2</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">accessKeyId</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{env.AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">secretAccessKey</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{env.AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">sessionToken</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{env.AWS_SESSION_TOKEN}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional, for temporary credentials</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">region</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;us-east-1&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional, defaults to us-east-1</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><strong>Environment variables:</strong></p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;your_access_key_id&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;your_secret_access_key&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">AWS_SESSION_TOKEN</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;your_session_token&quot;</span><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-warning admonition_WCGJ alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>Security Best Practice</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p><strong>Do not commit credentials to version control.</strong> Use environment variables or a dedicated secrets management system to handle sensitive keys.</p></div></div>
<p>This method overrides all other credential sources, including EC2 instance roles and SSO profiles.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="2-api-key-authentication">2. API Key authentication<a href="#2-api-key-authentication" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to 2. API Key authentication" title="Direct link to 2. API Key authentication" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>Amazon Bedrock API keys provide simplified authentication without managing AWS IAM credentials.</p>
<p><strong>Using environment variables:</strong></p>
<p>Set the <code>AWS_BEARER_TOKEN_BEDROCK</code> environment variable:</p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">AWS_BEARER_TOKEN_BEDROCK</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;your-api-key-here&quot;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us.anthropic.claude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">3</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20241022</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v2</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">region</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;us-east-1&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional, defaults to us-east-1</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><strong>Using config file:</strong></p>
<p>Specify the API key directly in your configuration:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20241022</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v2</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">apiKey</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;your-api-key-here&#x27;</span><span class="token class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional, defaults to us-east-1</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_WCGJ alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>API keys are limited to Amazon Bedrock and Amazon Bedrock Runtime actions. They cannot be used with:</p><ul>
<li class="">InvokeModelWithBidirectionalStream operations</li>
<li class="">Agents for Amazon Bedrock API operations</li>
<li class="">Data Automation for Amazon Bedrock API operations</li>
</ul><p>For these advanced features, use traditional AWS IAM credentials instead.</p></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="3-sso-profile-authentication">3. SSO profile authentication<a href="#3-sso-profile-authentication" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to 3. SSO profile authentication" title="Direct link to 3. SSO profile authentication" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>Use a named profile from your AWS configuration for AWS SSO setups or managing multiple AWS accounts:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us.anthropic.claude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">3</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20241022</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v2</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">profile</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;YOUR_SSO_PROFILE&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">region</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;us-east-1&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional, defaults to us-east-1</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><strong>Prerequisites for SSO profiles:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li class="">
<p><strong>Install AWS CLI v2</strong>: Ensure AWS CLI v2 is installed and on your PATH.</p>
</li>
<li class="">
<p><strong>Configure AWS SSO</strong>: Set up AWS SSO using the AWS CLI:</p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">aws configure sso</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
</li>
<li class="">
<p><strong>Profile configuration</strong>: Your <code>~/.aws/config</code> should contain the profile:</p>
<div class="language-ini codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-ini codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">[profile YOUR_SSO_PROFILE]</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">sso_start_url = https://your-sso-portal.awsapps.com/start</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">sso_region = us-east-1</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">sso_account_id = 123456789012</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">sso_role_name = YourRoleName</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">region = us-east-1</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
</li>
<li class="">
<p><strong>Active SSO session</strong>: Ensure you have an active SSO session:</p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">aws sso login </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:#36acaa">--profile</span><span class="token plain"> YOUR_SSO_PROFILE</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>Use SSO profiles when:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="">Managing multi-account AWS environments</li>
<li class="">Working in organizations with centralized AWS SSO</li>
<li class="">Your team needs different role-based permissions</li>
<li class="">You need to switch between different AWS contexts</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="4-default-credentials-lowest-priority">4. Default credentials (lowest priority)<a href="#4-default-credentials-lowest-priority" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to 4. Default credentials (lowest priority)" title="Direct link to 4. Default credentials (lowest priority)" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>Use the AWS SDK&#x27;s standard credential chain:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us.anthropic.claude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">3</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20241022</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v2</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">region</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;us-east-1&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Only region specified</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><strong>The AWS SDK checks these sources in order:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li class=""><strong>Environment variables</strong>: <code>AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID</code>, <code>AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY</code>, <code>AWS_SESSION_TOKEN</code></li>
<li class=""><strong>Shared credentials file</strong>: <code>~/.aws/credentials</code> (from <code>aws configure</code>)</li>
<li class=""><strong>AWS IAM roles</strong>: EC2 instance profiles, ECS task roles, Lambda execution roles</li>
<li class=""><strong>Shared AWS CLI credentials</strong>: Including cached SSO credentials</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>Use default credentials when:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="">Running on AWS infrastructure (EC2, ECS, Lambda) with IAM roles</li>
<li class="">Developing locally with AWS CLI configured (<code>aws configure</code>)</li>
<li class="">Working in CI/CD environments with IAM roles or environment variables</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Quick setup for local development:</strong></p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Option 1: Using AWS CLI</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">aws configure</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Option 2: Using environment variables</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;your_access_key&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;your_secret_key&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">AWS_DEFAULT_REGION</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;us-east-1&quot;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="example">Example<a href="#example" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Example" title="Direct link to Example" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>See <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/amazon-bedrock" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Github</a> for full examples of Claude, Nova, AI21, Llama 3.3, and Titan model usage.</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># yaml-language-server: $schema=https://promptfoo.dev/config-schema.json</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">prompts</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="model-specific-configuration">Model-specific Configuration<a href="#model-specific-configuration" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Model-specific Configuration" title="Direct link to Model-specific Configuration" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>Different models may support different configuration options. Here are some model-specific parameters:</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="general-configuration-options">General Configuration Options<a href="#general-configuration-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to General Configuration Options" title="Direct link to General Configuration Options" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>inferenceModelType</code>: (Required for inference profiles) Specifies the model family when using application inference profiles. Options include: <code>claude</code>, <code>nova</code>, <code>nova2</code>, <code>llama</code>, <code>llama2</code>, <code>llama3</code>, <code>llama3.1</code>, <code>llama3.2</code>, <code>llama3.3</code>, <code>llama4</code>, <code>mistral</code>, <code>cohere</code>, <code>ai21</code>, <code>titan</code>, <code>deepseek</code>, <code>openai</code>, <code>qwen</code></li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="amazon-nova-models">Amazon Nova Models<a href="#amazon-nova-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Amazon Nova Models" title="Direct link to Amazon Nova Models" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Amazon Nova models (e.g., <code>amazon.nova-lite-v1:0</code>, <code>amazon.nova-pro-v1:0</code>, <code>amazon.nova-micro-v1:0</code>, <code>amazon.nova-premier-v1:0</code>) support advanced features like tool use and structured outputs. You can configure them with the following options:</p>

<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_WCGJ alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Nova models use a slightly different configuration structure compared to other Bedrock models, with separate <code>interfaceConfig</code> and <code>toolConfig</code> sections.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="amazon-nova-2-models-reasoning">Amazon Nova 2 Models (Reasoning)<a href="#amazon-nova-2-models-reasoning" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Amazon Nova 2 Models (Reasoning)" title="Direct link to Amazon Nova 2 Models (Reasoning)" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Amazon Nova 2 models introduce extended thinking capabilities with configurable reasoning levels. Nova 2 Lite (<code>amazon.nova-2-lite-v1:0</code>) supports step-by-step reasoning and task decomposition with a 1 million token context window.</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Use cross-region model ID (us.) for on-demand access</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us.amazon.nova</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">2</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">lite</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v1</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">interfaceConfig</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_new_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">4096</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">reasoningConfig</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> enabled </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Enable extended thinking</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">maxReasoningEffort</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> medium </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># low, medium, or high</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><strong>Reasoning Configuration:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>type</code>: Set to <code>enabled</code> to activate extended thinking, or <code>disabled</code> for fast responses (default)</li>
<li class=""><code>maxReasoningEffort</code>: Controls thinking depth - <code>low</code>, <code>medium</code>, or <code>high</code></li>
</ul>
<p>When extended thinking is enabled, the model&#x27;s reasoning process is captured in the response output with <code>&lt;thinking&gt;</code> tags, similar to other reasoning models.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-warning admonition_WCGJ alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>warning</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>When using <code>reasoningConfig</code> with <code>type: enabled</code>:</p><ul>
<li class=""><strong>For all reasoning modes</strong>: Do not set <code>temperature</code>, <code>top_p</code>, or <code>top_k</code> - these are incompatible with reasoning mode</li>
<li class=""><strong>For <code>maxReasoningEffort: high</code></strong>: Also do not set <code>max_new_tokens</code> - the model manages output length automatically</li>
</ul></div></div>
<p><strong>Regional Model IDs:</strong></p>
<p>Nova 2 models require cross-region inference profiles for on-demand access:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>us.amazon.nova-2-lite-v1:0</code> - US region (recommended)</li>
<li class=""><code>eu.amazon.nova-2-lite-v1:0</code> - EU region</li>
<li class=""><code>apac.amazon.nova-2-lite-v1:0</code> - Asia Pacific region</li>
<li class=""><code>global.amazon.nova-2-lite-v1:0</code> - Global cross-region inference</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Using Nova 2 with Converse API:</strong></p>
<p>Nova 2 reasoning is also supported via the Converse API, which provides a unified interface across Bedrock models:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">converse</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us.amazon.nova</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">2</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">lite</span><span class="token style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">maxTokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">4096</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">reasoningConfig</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> enabled</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">maxReasoningEffort</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> medium</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The same parameter constraints apply when using the Converse API.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="amazon-nova-sonic-model">Amazon Nova Sonic Model<a href="#amazon-nova-sonic-model" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Amazon Nova Sonic Model" title="Direct link to Amazon Nova Sonic Model" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>The Amazon Nova Sonic model (<code>amazon.nova-sonic-v1:0</code>) is a multimodal model that supports audio input and text/audio output with tool-using capabilities. It has a different configuration structure compared to other Nova models:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" <p>Note: Nova Sonic has advanced multimodal capabilities including audio input/output, but audio input requires base64 encoded data which may be better handled through the API directly rather than in the configuration file.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="ai21-models">AI21 Models<a href="#ai21-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to AI21 Models" title="Direct link to AI21 Models" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="claude-models">Claude Models<a href="#claude-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Claude Models" title="Direct link to Claude Models" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>For Claude models (e.g., <code>anthropic.claude-sonnet-4-5-20250929-v1:0</code>, <code>anthropic.claude-haiku-4-5-20251001-v1:0</code>, <code>anthropic.claude-sonnet-4-20250514-v1:0</code>, <code>anthropic.us.claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022-v2:0</code>), you can use the following configuration options:</p>
<p><strong>Note</strong>: Claude Opus 4.5 (<code>anthropic.claude-opus-4-5-20251101-v1:0</code>) requires an inference profile ARN and cannot be used as a direct model ID. See the <a href="#application-inference-profiles" class="">Application Inference Profiles</a> section for setup.</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">...</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional: Specify available tools</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tool_choice</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">...</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional: Specify tool choice</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">thinking</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">...</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional: Enable Claude&#x27;s extended thinking capability</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">showThinking</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean important" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional: Control whether thinking content is included in output</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>When using Claude&#x27;s extended thinking capability, you can configure it like this:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">20000</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">thinking</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;enabled&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">budget_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">16000</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Must be â‰¥1024 and less than max_tokens</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">showThinking</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean important" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Whether to include thinking content in the output (default: true)</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_WCGJ alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>tip</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>The <code>showThinking</code> parameter controls whether thinking content is included in the response output:</p><ul>
<li class="">When set to <code>true</code> (default), thinking content will be included in the output</li>
<li class="">When set to <code>false</code>, thinking content will be excluded from the output</li>
</ul><p>This is useful when you want to use thinking for better reasoning but don&#x27;t want to expose the thinking process to end users.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="titan-models">Titan Models<a href="#titan-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Titan Models" title="Direct link to Titan Models" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>For Titan models (e.g., <code>amazon.titan-text-express-v1</code>), you can use the following configuration options:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="llama">Llama<a href="#llama" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Llama" title="Direct link to Llama" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
