<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="cohere-models">Cohere Models<a href="#cohere-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Cohere Models" title="Direct link to Cohere Models" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>For Cohere models (e.g., <code>cohere.command-text-v14</code>), you can use the following configuration options:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">256</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">p</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.9</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">k</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">stop_sequences</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;END&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="mistral-models">Mistral Models<a href="#mistral-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Mistral Models" title="Direct link to Mistral Models" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>For Mistral models (e.g., <code>mistral.mistral-7b-instruct-v0:2</code>), you can use the following configuration options:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">256</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">top_p</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.9</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">top_k</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">50</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="deepseek-models">DeepSeek Models<a href="#deepseek-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to DeepSeek Models" title="Direct link to DeepSeek Models" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>For DeepSeek models, you can use the following configuration options:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Deepseek params</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">256</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">top_p</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.9</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Promptfoo control params</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">showThinking</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean important" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional: Control whether thinking content is included in output</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>DeepSeek models support an extended thinking capability. The <code>showThinking</code> parameter controls whether thinking content is included in the response output:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">When set to <code>true</code> (default), thinking content will be included in the output</li>
<li class="">When set to <code>false</code>, thinking content will be excluded from the output</li>
</ul>
<p>This allows you to access the model&#x27;s reasoning process during generation while having the option to present only the final response to end users.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="openai-models">OpenAI Models<a href="#openai-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to OpenAI Models" title="Direct link to OpenAI Models" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>OpenAI&#x27;s open-weight models are available through AWS Bedrock with full support for their reasoning capabilities and parameters. The available models include:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong><code>openai.gpt-oss-120b-1:0</code></strong>: 120 billion parameter model with strong reasoning capabilities</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>openai.gpt-oss-20b-1:0</code></strong>: 20 billion parameter model, more cost-effective</li>
</ul>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_completion_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Controls randomness (0.0 to 1.0)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">top_p</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.9</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Nucleus sampling parameter</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.1</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Reduces repetition of frequent tokens</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">presence_penalty</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.1</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Reduces repetition of any tokens</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">stop</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;END&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;STOP&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Stop sequences</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">reasoning_effort</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;medium&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Controls reasoning depth: &#x27;low&#x27;, &#x27;medium&#x27;, &#x27;high&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="reasoning-effort">Reasoning Effort<a href="#reasoning-effort" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Reasoning Effort" title="Direct link to Reasoning Effort" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>OpenAI models support adjustable reasoning effort through the <code>reasoning_effort</code> parameter:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong><code>low</code></strong>: Faster responses with basic reasoning</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>medium</code></strong>: Balanced performance and reasoning depth</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>high</code></strong>: Thorough reasoning, slower but more accurate responses</li>
</ul>
<p>The reasoning effort is implemented via system prompt instructions, allowing the model to adjust its cognitive processing depth.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="usage-example">Usage Example<a href="#usage-example" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Usage Example" title="Direct link to Usage Example" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;high&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span <div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_WCGJ alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>OpenAI models use <code>max_completion_tokens</code> instead of <code>max_tokens</code> like other Bedrock models. This aligns with OpenAI&#x27;s API specification and allows for more precise control over response length.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="qwen-models">Qwen Models<a href="#qwen-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Qwen Models" title="Direct link to Qwen Models" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Alibaba&#x27;s Qwen models (e.g., <code>qwen.qwen3-coder-480b-a35b-v1:0</code>, <code>qwen.qwen3-coder-30b-a3b-v1:0</code>, <code>qwen.qwen3-235b-a22b-2507-v1:0</code>, <code>qwen.qwen3-32b-v1:0</code>) support advanced features including hybrid thinking modes, tool calling, and extended context understanding.</p>
<p><strong>Regional Availability</strong>: Check the <a href="https://console.aws.amazon.com/bedrock/home" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">AWS Bedrock console</a> or use <code>aws bedrock list-foundation-models</code> to verify which Qwen models are available in your target region, as availability varies by model and region.</p>
<p>You can configure them with the following options:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">2048</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Maximum number of tokens to generate</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Controls randomness (0.0 to 1.0)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">top_p</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.9</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Nucleus sampling parameter</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">frequency_penalty</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.1</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Reduces repetition of frequent tokens</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">presence_penalty</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.1</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Reduces repetition of any tokens</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">stop</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;END&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;STOP&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Stop sequences</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">showThinking</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean important" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Control whether thinking content is included in output</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tools</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">...</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Tool calling configuration (optional)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tool_choice</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;auto&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Tool selection strategy (optional)</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="hybrid-thinking-modes">Hybrid Thinking Modes<a href="#hybrid-thinking-modes" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Hybrid Thinking Modes" title="Direct link to Hybrid Thinking Modes" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>Qwen models support hybrid thinking modes where the model can apply step-by-step reasoning before delivering the final answer. The <code>showThinking</code> parameter controls whether thinking content is included in the response output:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">When set to <code>true</code> (default), thinking content will be included in the output</li>
<li class="">When set to <code>false</code>, thinking content will be excluded from the output</li>
</ul>
<p>This allows you to access the model&#x27;s reasoning process during generation while having the option to present only the final response to end users.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="tool-calling-support">Tool Calling Support<a href="#tool-calling-support" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Tool Calling Support" title="Direct link to Tool Calling Support" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>Qwen models support tool calling with OpenAI-compatible function definitions:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" name</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="model-variants">Model Variants<a href="#model-variants" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Model Variants" title="Direct link to Model Variants" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Qwen3-Coder-480B-A35B</strong>: Mixture-of-experts model optimized for coding and agentic tasks with 480B total parameters and 35B active parameters</li>
<li class=""><strong>Qwen3-Coder-30B-A3B</strong>: Smaller MoE model with 30B total parameters and 3B active parameters, optimized for coding tasks</li>
<li class=""><strong>Qwen3-235B-A22B</strong>: General-purpose MoE model with 235B total parameters and 22B active parameters for reasoning and coding</li>
<li class=""><strong>Qwen3-32B</strong>: Dense model with 32B parameters for consistent performance in resource-constrained environments</li>
</ul>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="model-graded-tests">Model-graded tests<a href="#model-graded-tests" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Model-graded tests" title="Direct link to Model-graded tests" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>You can use Bedrock models to grade outputs. By default, model-graded tests use <code>gpt-5</code> and require the <code>OPENAI_API_KEY</code> environment variable to be set. However, when using AWS Bedrock, you have the option of overriding the grader for <a class="" href="/docs/configuration/expected-outputs/model-graded/">model-graded assertions</a> to point to AWS Bedrock or other providers.</p>
<p>You can use either regular model IDs or application inference profiles for grading:</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-warning admonition_WCGJ alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>warning</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Because of how model-graded evals are implemented, <strong>the LLM grading models must support chat-formatted prompts</strong> (except for embedding or classification models).</p></div></div>
<p>To set this for all your test cases, add the <a class="" href="/docs/configuration/guide/#default-test-cases"><code>defaultTest</code></a> property to your config:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">defaultTest</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">options</span><span class="token atrule" style="color:#00a4db">provider</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Using a regular model ID</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us.anthropic.claude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">3</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20241022</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v2</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Other provider config options</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Or using an inference profile</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># id: bedrock:arn:aws:bedrock:us-east-1:123456789012:application-inference-profile/grading-profile</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># config:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">#   inferenceModelType: &#x27;claude&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">#   temperature: 0</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>You can also do this for individual assertions:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># ...</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> llm</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">rubric</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> Do not mention that you are an AI or chat assistant</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">provider</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" <p>Or for individual tests:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="multimodal-capabilities">Multimodal Capabilities<a href="#multimodal-capabilities" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Multimodal Capabilities" title="Direct link to Multimodal Capabilities" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>Several Bedrock models support multimodal inputs including images and text:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Amazon Nova</strong> - Supports images and videos</li>
<li class=""><strong>Llama 3.2 Vision</strong> - Supports images (11B and 90B variants)</li>
<li class=""><strong>Claude 3+</strong> - Supports images (via Converse API)</li>
<li class=""><strong>Pixtral Large</strong> - Supports images (via Converse API)</li>
</ul>
<p>To use these capabilities, structure your prompts to include both image data and text content.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="nova-vision-capabilities">Nova Vision Capabilities<a href="#nova-vision-capabilities" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Nova Vision Capabilities" title="Direct link to Nova Vision Capabilities" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Amazon Nova supports comprehensive vision understanding for both images and videos:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Images</strong>: Supports PNG, JPG, JPEG, GIF, WebP formats via Base-64 encoding. Multiple images allowed per payload (up to 25MB total).</li>
<li class=""><strong>Videos</strong>: Supports various formats (MP4, MKV, MOV, WEBM, etc.) via Base-64 (less than 25MB) or Amazon S3 URI (up to 1GB).</li>
</ul>
<p>Here&#x27;s an example configuration for running multimodal evaluations:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span <p>The prompt file (<code>nova_multimodal_prompt.json</code>) should be structured to include both image and text content. This format will depend on the specific model you&#x27;re using:</p>

<p>See <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/blob/main/examples/amazon-bedrock/promptfooconfig.nova.multimodal.yaml" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Github</a> for a runnable example.</p>
<p>When loading image files as variables, Promptfoo automatically converts them to the appropriate format for the model. The supported image formats include:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">jpg/jpeg</li>
<li class="">png</li>
<li class="">gif</li>
<li class="">bmp</li>
<li class="">webp</li>
<li class="">svg</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="embeddings">Embeddings<a href="#embeddings" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Embeddings" title="Direct link to Embeddings" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>To override the embeddings provider for all assertions that require embeddings (such as similarity), use <code>defaultTest</code>:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="guardrails">Guardrails<a href="#guardrails" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Guardrails" title="Direct link to Guardrails" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>To use guardrails, set the <code>guardrailIdentifier</code> and <code>guardrailVersion</code> in the provider config.</p>
<p>For example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us.anthropic.claude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">3</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20241022</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v2</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">guardrailIdentifier</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;test-guardrail&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">guardrailVersion</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># The version number for the guardrail. The value can also be DRAFT.</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="environment-variables">Environment Variables<a href="#environment-variables" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Environment Variables" title="Direct link to Environment Variables" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>The following environment variables can be used to configure the Bedrock provider:</p>
<p><strong>Authentication:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>AWS_BEARER_TOKEN_BEDROCK</code>: Bedrock API key for simplified authentication</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Configuration:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>AWS_BEDROCK_REGION</code>: Default region for Bedrock API calls</li>
<li class=""><code>AWS_BEDROCK_MAX_TOKENS</code>: Default maximum number of tokens to generate</li>
<li class=""><code>AWS_BEDROCK_TEMPERATURE</code>: Default temperature for generation</li>
<li class=""><code>AWS_BEDROCK_TOP_P</code>: Default top_p value for generation</li>
<li class=""><code>AWS_BEDROCK_FREQUENCY_PENALTY</code>: Default frequency penalty (for supported models)</li>
<li class=""><code>AWS_BEDROCK_PRESENCE_PENALTY</code>: Default presence penalty (for supported models)</li>
<li class=""><code>AWS_BEDROCK_STOP</code>: Default stop sequences (as a JSON string)</li>
<li class=""><code>AWS_BEDROCK_MAX_RETRIES</code>: Number of retry attempts for failed API calls (default: 10)</li>
</ul>
<p>Model-specific environment variables:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>MISTRAL_MAX_TOKENS</code>, <code>MISTRAL_TEMPERATURE</code>, <code>MISTRAL_TOP_P</code>, <code>MISTRAL_TOP_K</code>: For Mistral models</li>
<li class=""><code>COHERE_TEMPERATURE</code>, <code>COHERE_P</code>, <code>COHERE_K</code>, <code>COHERE_MAX_TOKENS</code>: For Cohere models</li>
</ul>
<p>These environment variables can be overridden by the configuration specified in the YAML file.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="troubleshooting">Troubleshooting<a href="#troubleshooting" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Troubleshooting" title="Direct link to Troubleshooting" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="authentication-issues">Authentication Issues<a href="#authentication-issues" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Authentication Issues" title="Direct link to Authentication Issues" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="unable-to-locate-credentials-error">&quot;Unable to locate credentials&quot; Error<a href="#unable-to-locate-credentials-error" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to &quot;Unable to locate credentials&quot; Error" title="Direct link to &quot;Unable to locate credentials&quot; Error" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<div class="language-text codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">Error: Unable to locate credentials. You can configure credentials by running &quot;aws configure&quot;.</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li class=""><strong>Check credential priority</strong>: Ensure credentials are available in the expected priority order</li>
<li class=""><strong>Verify AWS CLI setup</strong>: Run <code>aws configure list</code> to see active credentials</li>
<li class=""><strong>SSO session expired</strong>: Run <code>aws sso login --profile YOUR_PROFILE</code></li>
<li class=""><strong>Environment variables</strong>: Verify <code>AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID</code> and <code>AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY</code> are set</li>
</ol>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="accessdenied-or-unauthorizedoperation-errors">&quot;AccessDenied&quot; or &quot;UnauthorizedOperation&quot; Errors<a href="#accessdenied-or-unauthorizedoperation-errors" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to &quot;AccessDenied&quot; or &quot;UnauthorizedOperation&quot; Errors" title="Direct link to &quot;AccessDenied&quot; or &quot;UnauthorizedOperation&quot; Errors" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li class=""><strong>Check IAM permissions</strong>: Ensure your credentials have <code>bedrock:InvokeModel</code> permission</li>
<li class=""><strong>Model access</strong>: Enable model access in the AWS Bedrock console</li>
<li class=""><strong>Region mismatch</strong>: Verify the region in your config matches where you enabled model access</li>
</ol>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="sso-specific-issues">SSO-Specific Issues<a href="#sso-specific-issues" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to SSO-Specific Issues" title="Direct link to SSO-Specific Issues" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p><strong>&quot;SSO session has expired&quot;:</strong></p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">aws sso login </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:#36acaa">--profile</span><span class="token plain"> YOUR_PROFILE</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><strong>&quot;Profile not found&quot;:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="">Check <code>~/.aws/config</code> contains the profile</li>
<li class="">Verify profile name matches exactly (case-sensitive)</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="debugging-authentication">Debugging Authentication<a href="#debugging-authentication" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Debugging Authentication" title="Direct link to Debugging Authentication" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>Enable debug logging to see which credentials are being used:</p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">AWS_SDK_JS_LOG</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">npx promptfoo </span><span class="token builtin class-name">eval</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>This will show detailed AWS SDK logs including credential resolution.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="model-configuration-issues">Model Configuration Issues<a href="#model-configuration-issues" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Model Configuration Issues" title="Direct link to Model Configuration Issues" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="inference-profile-requires-inferencemodeltype">Inference profile requires inferenceModelType<a href="#inference-profile-requires-inferencemodeltype" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Inference profile requires inferenceModelType" title="Direct link to Inference profile requires inferenceModelType" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>If you see this error when using an inference profile ARN:</p>
<div class="language-text codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">Error: Inference profile requires inferenceModelType to be specified in config. Options: claude, nova, llama (defaults to v4), llama2, llama3, llama3.1, llama3.2, llama3.3, llama4, mistral, cohere, ai21, titan, deepseek, openai, qwen</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>This means you&#x27;re using an application inference profile ARN but haven&#x27;t specified which model family it&#x27;s configured for. Add the <code>inferenceModelType</code> to your configuration:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">arn</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">aws</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">east</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">1</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">123456789012</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">application</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token class="token plain">profile</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">inferenceModelType</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;claude&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Specify the model family</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="validationexception-on-demand-throughput-isnt-supported">ValidationException: On-demand throughput isn&#x27;t supported<a href="#validationexception-on-demand-throughput-isnt-supported" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to ValidationException: On-demand throughput isn&#x27;t supported" title="Direct link to ValidationException: On-demand throughput isn&#x27;t supported" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>If you see this error:</p>
<div class="language-text codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">ValidationException: Invocation of model ID anthropic.claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022-v2:0 with on-demand throughput isn&#x27;t supported. Retry your request with the ID or ARN of an inference profile that contains this model.</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>This usually means you need to use the region-specific model ID. Update your provider configuration to include the regional prefix:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Use this:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">4</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20250929</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v1</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># US region</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># or</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">eu.anthropic.claude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">4</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20250929</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v1</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># EU region</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># or</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">apac.anthropic.claude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">4</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20250929</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v1</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># APAC region</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Make sure to:</p>
<ol>
<li class="">Choose the correct regional prefix (<code>us.</code>, <code>eu.</code>, or <code>apac.</code>) based on your AWS region</li>
<li class="">Configure the corresponding region in your provider config</li>
<li class="">Ensure you have model access enabled in your AWS Bedrock console for that region</li>
</ol>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="accessdeniedexception-you-dont-have-access-to-the-model-with-the-specified-model-id">AccessDeniedException: You don&#x27;t have access to the model with the specified model ID<a href="#accessdeniedexception-you-dont-have-access-to-the-model-with-the-specified-model-id" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to AccessDeniedException: You don&#x27;t have access to the model with the specified model ID" title="Direct link to AccessDeniedException: You don&#x27;t have access to the model with the specified model ID" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>If you see this error, the cause depends on which model provider you&#x27;re using:</p>
<p><strong>For most serverless models</strong> (Amazon, DeepSeek, Mistral, Meta, Qwen, OpenAI):</p>
<ul>
<li class="">These models have instant access with no approval required</li>
<li class="">Verify your IAM permissions include <code>bedrock:InvokeModel</code></li>
<li class="">Check your region configuration matches the model&#x27;s region</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>For Anthropic models (Claude)</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">First-time use requires submitting use case details in the Bedrock console</li>
<li class="">Access is granted immediately after submission</li>
<li class="">This is a one-time step per AWS account or organization</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>For AWS Marketplace models</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Ensure your IAM permissions include <code>aws-marketplace:Subscribe</code></li>
<li class="">Subscribe to the model through AWS Marketplace</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="knowledge-base">Knowledge Base<a href="#knowledge-base" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Knowledge Base" title="Direct link to Knowledge Base" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>AWS Bedrock Knowledge Bases provide Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) functionality, allowing you to query a knowledge base with natural language and get responses based on your data.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="prerequisites">Prerequisites<a href="#prerequisites" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Prerequisites" title="Direct link to Prerequisites" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>To use the Knowledge Base provider, you need:</p>
<ol>
<li class="">
<p>An existing Knowledge Base created in AWS Bedrock</p>
</li>
<li class="">
<p>Install the <code>@aws-sdk/client-bedrock-agent-runtime</code> package:</p>
<div class="language-sh codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-sh codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">npm</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">install</span><span class="token plain"> @aws-sdk/client-bedrock-agent-runtime</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="configuration">Configuration<a href="#configuration" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Configuration" title="Direct link to Configuration" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Configure the Knowledge Base provider by specifying <code>kb</code> in your provider ID. Note that the model ID needs to include the regional prefix (<code>us.</code>, <code>eu.</code>, or <code>apac.</code>):</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">kb</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">us.anthropic.claude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">3</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">7</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sonnet</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">20250219</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">v1</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">region</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;us-east-2&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">knowledgeBaseId</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;YOUR_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1000</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">numberOfResults</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">5</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional: number of chunks to retrieve (AWS default when not specified)</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The provider ID follows this pattern: <code>bedrock:kb:[REGIONAL_MODEL_ID]</code></p>
<p>For example:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>bedrock:kb:us.anthropic.claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022-v2:0</code> (US region)</li>
<li class=""><code>bedrock:kb:eu.anthropic.claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022-v2:0</code> (EU region)</li>
</ul>
<p>Configuration options include:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>knowledgeBaseId</code> (required): The ID of your AWS Bedrock Knowledge Base</li>
<li class=""><code>region</code>: AWS region where your Knowledge Base is deployed (e.g., &#x27;us-east-1&#x27;, &#x27;us-east-2&#x27;, &#x27;eu-west-1&#x27;)</li>
<li class=""><code>temperature</code>: Controls randomness in response generation (default: 0.0)</li>
<li class=""><code>max_tokens</code>: Maximum number of tokens in the generated response</li>
<li class=""><code>numberOfResults</code>: Number of chunks to retrieve from the knowledge base (optional, uses AWS default when not specified)</li>
<li class=""><code>accessKeyId</code>, <code>secretAccessKey</code>, <code>sessionToken</code>: AWS credentials (if not using environment variables or IAM roles)</li>
<li class=""><code>profile</code>: AWS profile name for SSO authentication</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="knowledge-base-example">Knowledge Base Example<a href="#knowledge-base-example" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Knowledge Base Example" title="Direct link to Knowledge Base Example" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="citations">Citations<a href="#citations" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Citations" title="Direct link to Citations" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>The Knowledge Base provider returns both the generated response and citations from the source documents. These citations are included in the evaluation results and can be used to verify the accuracy of the responses.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_WCGJ alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>info</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>When viewing evaluation results in the UI, citations appear in a separate section within the details view of each response. You can click on the source links to visit the original documents or copy citation content for reference.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="response-format">Response Format<a href="#response-format" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Response Format" title="Direct link to Response Format" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>When using the Knowledge Base provider, the response will include:</p>
<ol>
<li class=""><strong>output</strong>: The text response generated by the model based on your query</li>
<li class=""><strong>metadata.citations</strong>: An array of citations that includes:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li class=""><code>retrievedReferences</code>: References to source documents that informed the response</li>
<li class=""><code>generatedResponsePart</code>: Parts of the response that correspond to specific citations</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="context-evaluation-with-contexttransform">Context Evaluation with contextTransform<a href="#context-evaluation-with-contexttransform" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Context Evaluation with contextTransform" title="Direct link to Context Evaluation with contextTransform" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>The Knowledge Base provider supports extracting context from citations for evaluation using the <code>contextTransform</code> feature:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tests</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">vars</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">query</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;What is promptfoo?&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Extract context from all citations</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> context</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">faithfulness</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">contextTransform</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">|</span><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          if (!metadata?.citations) return &#x27;&#x27;;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          return metadata.citations</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            .flatMap(citation =&gt; citation.retrievedReferences || [])</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            .map(ref =&gt; ref.content?.text || &#x27;&#x27;)</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            .filter(text =&gt; text.length &gt; 0)</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            .join(&#x27;\n\n&#x27;);</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Extract context from first citation only</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> context</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">relevance</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">contextTransform</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;metadata?.citations?.[0]?.retrievedReferences?.[0]?.content?.text || &quot;&quot;&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.6</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>This approach allows you to:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Evaluate real retrieval</strong>: Test against the actual context retrieved by your Knowledge Base</li>
<li class=""><strong>Measure faithfulness</strong>: Verify responses don&#x27;t hallucinate beyond the retrieved content</li>
<li class=""><strong>Assess relevance</strong>: Check if retrieved context is relevant to the query</li>
<li class=""><strong>Validate recall</strong>: Ensure important information appears in retrieved context</li>
</ul>
<p>See the <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/amazon-bedrock" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Knowledge Base contextTransform example</a> for complete configuration examples.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="bedrock-agents">Bedrock Agents<a href="#bedrock-agents" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Bedrock Agents" title="Direct link to Bedrock Agents" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>Amazon Bedrock Agents uses the reasoning of foundation models (FMs), APIs, and data to break down user requests, gathers relevant information, and efficiently completes tasksâ€”freeing teams to focus on high-value work. For detailed information on testing and evaluating deployed agents, see the <a class="" href="/docs/providers/bedrock-agents/">AWS Bedrock Agents Provider</a> documentation.</p>
<p>Quick example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> bedrock</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">agent</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">YOUR_AGENT_ID</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">agentAliasId</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> PROD_ALIAS</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">region</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> us</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">east</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">enableTrace</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean important" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="see-also">See Also<a href="#see-also" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to See Also" title="Direct link to See Also" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class=""><a class="" href="/docs/providers/sagemaker/">Amazon SageMaker Provider</a> - For custom-deployed or fine-tuned models on AWS</li>
<li class=""><a class="" href="/docs/guides/evaluate-rag/">RAG Evaluation Guide</a> - Complete guide to evaluating RAG systems with context-based assertions</li>
<li class=""><a class="" href="/docs/configuration/expected-outputs/model-graded/">Context-based Assertions</a> - Documentation on context-faithfulness, context-relevance, and context-recall</li>
<li class=""><a class="" href="/docs/configuration/reference/">Configuration Reference</a> - Complete configuration options including contextTransform</li>
<li class=""><a class="" href="/docs/usage/command-line/">Command Line Interface</a> - How to use promptfoo from the command line</li>
<li class=""><a class="" href="/docs/providers/">Provider Options</a> - Overview of all supported providers</li>
<li class=""><a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/amazon-bedrock" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Amazon Bedrock Examples</a> - Runnable examples of Bedrock integration, including Knowledge Base and contextTransform examples</li>
